<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript" data-rocket-src="https://www.webdo.tn/fr/wp-includes/js/jquery/jquery.min.js?ver=3.7.1" id="jquery-core-js" data-rocket-defer defer></script>
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript" data-rocket-src="https://www.webdo.tn/fr/wp-includes/js/jquery/jquery-migrate.min.js?ver=3.4.1" id="jquery-migrate-js" data-rocket-defer defer></script>
<link rel="https://api.w.org/" href="https://www.webdo.tn/fr/wp-json/" /><link rel="alternate" title="JSON" type="application/json" href="https://www.webdo.tn/fr/wp-json/wp/v2/pages/232638" /><link rel="EditURI" type="application/rsd+xml" title="RSD" href="https://www.webdo.tn/fr/xmlrpc.php?rsd" />
<meta name="generator" content="WordPress 6.9.1" />
<link rel='shortlink' href='https://www.webdo.tn/fr/' />
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
(function () {

    /* ===============================
     * Liste pays UE
     * =============================== */
    var EU = [
        "FR","BE","DE","IT","ES","NL","AT","IE","LU","SE","FI","PT","GR","CY","MT",
        "DK","CZ","PL","HU","RO","BG","SK","SI","HR","EE","LV","LT","IS","NO","LI"
    ];

    function isEU(code) {
        return code && EU.indexOf(code.toUpperCase()) !== -1;
    }

    /* ===============================
     * Garantir gtag
     * =============================== */
    function ensureGtag() {
        if (!window.dataLayer) window.dataLayer = [];
        if (typeof window.gtag !== "function") {
            window.gtag = function () { window.dataLayer.push(arguments); };
        }
    }

    /* ===============================
     * Consentements
     * =============================== */
    function consentFull(reason) {
        window.gtag('consent', 'update', {
            ad_storage: 'granted',
            analytics_storage: 'granted',
            personalization_storage: 'granted',
            security_storage: 'granted',
            functionality_storage: 'granted'
        });
        console.log('[Webdo RGPD] FULL → ' + reason);
    }

    function consentEU() {
        window.gtag('consent', 'update', {
            ad_storage: 'granted',
            analytics_storage: 'granted',
            personalization_storage: 'denied',
            security_storage: 'granted',
            functionality_storage: 'granted'
        });
        console.log('[Webdo RGPD] UE → ads limitées');
    }

    /* ===============================
     * Bandeau consentement
     * =============================== */
    function showBanner() {
        if (document.getElementById('webdo-consent-banner')) return;

        var bar = document.createElement('div');
        bar.id = 'webdo-consent-banner';
        bar.style.cssText =
            "position:fixed;left:0;right:0;bottom:0;z-index:99999;" +
            "background:rgba(0,0,0,.85);color:#fff;padding:10px 16px;" +
            "display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;" +
            "font-size:13px;";

        var text = document.createElement('div');
        text.textContent = "Ce site utilise des cookies à des fins de mesure et de publicité.";

        var btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.textContent = "OK";
        btn.style.cssText =
            "background:#00c853;border:none;color:#fff;padding:6px 14px;" +
            "border-radius:4px;cursor:pointer;margin-left:10px;";

        btn.onclick = function () {
            localStorage.setItem('webdo_consent_ok', '1');
            consentFull("EU: user accepted");
            bar.style.opacity = '0';
            setTimeout(function () { bar.remove(); }, 300);
        };

        bar.appendChild(text);
        bar.appendChild(btn);
        document.body.appendChild(bar);
    }

    /* ===============================
     * Consentement par défaut (FULL)
     * =============================== */
    ensureGtag();
    window.gtag('consent', 'default', {
        ad_storage: 'granted',
        analytics_storage: 'granted',
        personalization_storage: 'granted',
        security_storage: 'granted',
        functionality_storage: 'granted'
    });
    console.log('[Webdo RGPD] DEFAULT FULL');

    /* ===============================
     * Logique RGPD (exécutée en idle)
     * =============================== */
    function webdoRunRGPD() {

        var done = false;
        function mark() {
            if (done) return true;
            done = true;
            return false;
        }

        var timer = setTimeout(function () {
            if (mark()) return;
            console.log('[Webdo RGPD] timeout → FULL');
        }, 1200);

        fetch("https://api.country.is/")
            .then(function (r) { return r.json(); })
            .then(function (data) {

                if (mark()) return;
                clearTimeout(timer);

                var code = data.country || "";

                if (!isEU(code)) {
                    console.log("[Webdo RGPD] NON-UE (" + code + ") → FULL");
                    return;
                }

                console.log("[Webdo RGPD] UE (" + code + ")");

                var ok = (localStorage.getItem('webdo_consent_ok') === "1");

                if (ok) {
                    consentFull("EU stored");
                } else {
                    consentEU();
                    showBanner();
                }
            })
            .catch(function () {
                if (mark()) return;
                clearTimeout(timer);
                console.log("[Webdo RGPD] Geo error → FULL");
            });
    }

    /* ===============================
     * Lancement INP-safe
     * =============================== */
    if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
        requestIdleCallback(webdoRunRGPD, { timeout: 2000 });
    } else {
        setTimeout(webdoRunRGPD, 1200);
    }

})();
</script>

               : path.indexOf('/en/') === 0 || path === '/en' ? 'en'
               : 'fr';
    toggle.setAttribute('data-active-lang', active);

    // Conserve le reste du chemin (suppose mêmes slugs entre langues)
    var rest = path.replace(/^\/(en|ar)(\/|$)/, '/');

    var linkFr = toggle.querySelector('.lang-option.fr');
    var linkAr = toggle.querySelector('.lang-option.ar');
    var linkEn = toggle.querySelector('.lang-option.en');
    if (linkFr) linkFr.setAttribute('href', base + rest);
    if (linkAr) linkAr.setAttribute('href', base + '/ar' + rest);
    if (linkEn) linkEn.setAttribute('href', base + '/en' + rest);

    // Pas de délai/animation bloquante : on laisse la navigation se faire
    toggle.querySelectorAll('.lang-option').forEach(function(a){
      a.addEventListener('click', function(){ /* accessibilité: rien à empêcher */ });
      // aria-current pour l’état actif
      a.setAttribute('aria-current', a.getAttribute('data-lang') === active ? 'true' : 'false');

  })();

    <div class="lang-toggle" data-active-lang="" aria-label="Language switcher">
  <a class="lang-option fr" href="/fr/" data-lang="fr" lang="fr" hreflang="fr" aria-label="Français">🇫🇷 <span class="abbr">FR</span></a>
  <a class="lang-option ar" href="/ar/" data-lang="ar" lang="ar" hreflang="ar" aria-label="العربية">🇸🇦 <span class="abbr">AR</span></a>
  <a class="lang-option en" href="/en/" data-lang="en" lang="en" hreflang="en" aria-label="English">🇬🇧 <span class="abbr">EN</span></a>
  <span class="lang-slider"></span>
</div>

<div class="lang-dropdown" aria-label="Language switcher">
  <label for="lang-select" class="sr-only">Language</label>
  <select id="lang-select">
    <option value="fr">FR</option>

<style></style>

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
  (function() {
    var toggle = document.querySelector('.lang-toggle');
    if (!toggle) return;

    var base = 'https://www.webdo.tn'; // adapte si nécessaire
    var path = window.location.pathname || '/';
    var active = path.indexOf('/ar/') === 0 || path === '/ar' ? 'ar'
               : path.indexOf('/en/') === 0 || path === '/en' ? 'en'
               : 'fr';
    toggle.setAttribute('data-active-lang', active);

    // Conserve le reste du chemin (suppose mêmes slugs entre langues)
    var rest = path.replace(/^\/(en|ar)(\/|$)/, '/');

    var linkFr = toggle.querySelector('.lang-option.fr');
    var linkAr = toggle.querySelector('.lang-option.ar');
    var linkEn = toggle.querySelector('.lang-option.en');
    if (linkFr) linkFr.setAttribute('href', base + rest);
    if (linkAr) linkAr.setAttribute('href', base + '/ar' + rest);
    if (linkEn) linkEn.setAttribute('href', base + '/en' + rest);

    // Pas de délai/animation bloquante : on laisse la navigation se faire
    toggle.querySelectorAll('.lang-option').forEach(function(a){
      a.addEventListener('click', function(){ /* accessibilité: rien à empêcher */ });
      // aria-current pour l’état actif
      a.setAttribute('aria-current', a.getAttribute('data-lang') === active ? 'true' : 'false');
    });

    // Dropdown mobile: valeur active et redirection
    var hrefFr = base + rest;
    var hrefAr = base + '/ar' + rest;
    var hrefEn = base + '/en' + rest;
    var select = document.getElementById('lang-select');
    if (select) {
      select.value = active;
      select.addEventListener('change', function() {
        var value = select.value;
        var target = value === 'ar' ? hrefAr : (value === 'en' ? hrefEn : hrefFr);
        window.location.href = target;
      });
    }
  })();
</script></div>                    </div>
